    [CostCenter] int NOT NULL,
    [Category] int NOT NULL,
    [ExpenseType] int NOT NULL,
    [ExpenseDate] datetime2 NOT NULL,
    [InvoiceNumber] nvarchar(100) NOT NULL,
    [PurchaseOrderNumber] nvarchar(max) NULL,
    [InvoiceDate] datetime2 NULL,
    [DueDate] datetime2 NULL,
    [Currency] int NOT NULL,
    [Amount] decimal(18,2) NOT NULL,
    [TaxAmount] decimal(18,2) NOT NULL,
    [TaxPercentage] decimal(5,2) NOT NULL,
    [TotalAmount] decimal(18,2) NOT NULL,
    [PaymentStatus] int NOT NULL,
    [PaymentMethod] int NOT NULL,
    [Status] int NOT NULL,
    [Description] nvarchar(2000) NOT NULL,
    [Remarks] nvarchar(max) NULL,
    [IsDeleted] bit NOT NULL DEFAULT CAST(0 AS bit),
    [IsActive] bit NOT NULL DEFAULT CAST(1 AS bit),
    [IsRecurring] bit NOT NULL,
    [RecurringMonths] int NULL,
    [IsForecasted] bit NOT NULL,
    [CreatedOn] datetime2 NOT NULL DEFAULT (GETUTCDATE()),
    [UpdatedOn] datetime2 NULL,
    [CreatedBy] nvarchar(max) NULL,
    [UpdatedBy] nvarchar(max) NULL,
    [ContractId1] int NULL,
    [VendorId1] int NULL,
    CONSTRAINT [PK_Expenditures] PRIMARY KEY ([Id]),
    CONSTRAINT [FK_Expenditures_Contracts_ContractId] FOREIGN KEY ([ContractId]) REFERENCES [Contracts] ([Id]) ON DELETE NO ACTION,
    CONSTRAINT [FK_Expenditures_Contracts_ContractId1] FOREIGN KEY ([ContractId1]) REFERENCES [Contracts] ([Id]),
    CONSTRAINT [FK_Expenditures_Vendors_VendorId] FOREIGN KEY ([VendorId]) REFERENCES [Vendors] ([Id]) ON DELETE NO ACTION,

    [PurchaseOrderNumber] nvarchar(max) NULL,
    [InvoiceDate] datetime2 NULL,
    [DueDate] datetime2 NULL,
    [Currency] int NOT NULL,
    [Amount] decimal(18,2) NOT NULL,
    [TaxAmount] decimal(18,2) NOT NULL,
    [TaxPercentage] decimal(5,2) NOT NULL,
    [TotalAmount] decimal(18,2) NOT NULL,
    [PaymentStatus] int NOT NULL,
    [PaymentMethod] int NOT NULL,
    [Status] int NOT NULL,
    [Description] nvarchar(2000) NOT NULL,
    [Remarks] nvarchar(max) NULL,
    [IsDeleted] bit NOT NULL DEFAULT CAST(0 AS bit),
    [IsActive] bit NOT NULL DEFAULT CAST(1 AS bit),
    [IsRecurring] bit NOT NULL,
    [RecurringMonths] int NULL,
    [IsForecasted] bit NOT NULL,
    [CreatedOn] datetime2 NOT NULL DEFAULT (GETUTCDATE()),
    [UpdatedOn] datetime2 NULL,
    [CreatedBy] nvarchar(max) NULL,
    [UpdatedBy] nvarchar(max) NULL,
    [ContractId1] int NULL,
    [VendorId1] int NULL,
    CONSTRAINT [PK_Expenditures] PRIMARY KEY ([Id]),
    CONSTRAINT [FK_Expenditures_Contracts_ContractId] FOREIGN KEY ([ContractId]) REFERENCES [Contracts] ([Id]) ON DELETE NO ACTION,
    CONSTRAINT [FK_Expenditures_Contracts_ContractId1] FOREIGN KEY ([ContractId1]) REFERENCES [Contracts] ([Id]),

    WHERE [u].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [u0].[UserId], [u0].[RoleId], [u0].[AssignedBy], [u0].[AssignedOn], [r].[Id], [r].[Color], [r].[CreatedOn], [r].[Description], [r].[Icon], [r].[IsActive], [r].[IsDeleted], [r].[IsSystemRole], [r].[Name], [r].[Priority], [r].[UpdatedOn], [t1].[RoleId] AS [RoleId0], [t1].[PermissionId], [t1].[AssignedBy] AS [AssignedBy0], [t1].[AssignedOn] AS [AssignedOn0], [t1].[Id] AS [Id0], [t1].[Code], [t1].[CreatedOn] AS [CreatedOn0], [t1].[Description] AS [Description0], [t1].[IsActive] AS [IsActive0], [t1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted0], [t1].[Module], [t1].[Name] AS [Name0], [t1].[UpdatedOn] AS [UpdatedOn0]

    INNER JOIN [Roles] AS [r] ON [u0].[RoleId] = [r].[Id]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [r0].[RoleId], [r0].[PermissionId], [r0].[AssignedBy], [r0].[AssignedOn], [p].[Id], [p].[Code], [p].[CreatedOn], [p].[Description], [p].[IsActive], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[Module], [p].[Name], [p].[UpdatedOn]

) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[UserId]
